class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">1</span><h2 id="before-you-begin" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#before-you-begin" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#before-you-begin" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Before you begin</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3>Check your account setup for advanced card payments</h3><span>
</span><p><span>This integration requires a sandbox business account with the Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments capability. Your account should automatically have this capability.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>To confirm that Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments are enabled for you, check your sandbox business account as follows:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
</span><li><span>Log into the </span><a href="/dashboard/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><strong><span>PayPal Developer Dashboard</span></strong></a><span>, toggle </span><strong><span>Sandbox</span></strong><span>, and go to </span><strong><span>Apps & Credentials</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>In </span><strong><span>REST API apps</span></strong><span>, select the name of your app.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>Go to </span><strong><span>Features</span></strong><span> &gt; </span><strong><span>Accept payments</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>Select the </span><strong><span>Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments</span></strong><span> checkbox and select </span><strong><span>Save Changes</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><strong><span>Note:</span></strong><span> If you created a sandbox business account through </span><a href="https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/?_ga=1.158343865.248280996.1670866755" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>sandbox.paypal.com</span></a><span>, and the advanced credit and debit card payments status for the account is disabled, </span><a href="https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/bizsignup/#/checkAccount" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>complete the sandbox onboarding steps</span></a><span>.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3>Check 3D Secure requirements</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Add 3D Secure to reduce the chance of fraud and improve the payment experience by authenticating a cardholder through their card issuer.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Visit our </span><a href="/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/3d-secure/" target="_blank"><span>3D Secure</span></a><span> page to see if 3D Secure is required in your region and learn more about implementing 3D Secure in your app.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">2</span><h2 id="integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Integrate the SDK into your app</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Integrate 3 different types of payments using the PayPal Mobile SDK:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><strong><span>Card payments:</span></strong><span> Add card fields that align with your branding.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><strong><span>PayPal native payments:</span></strong><span> Launch a checkout page within your app, instead of a popup.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><strong><span>PayPal web payments:</span></strong><span> A lighter integration that launches a checkout page in a browser within your app.</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div </span><h2>Integrate with card payments</h2><span>
</span><p><span>Build and customize the card fields to align with your branding.</span></p><span>
</span><h3>1. Add card payments module to your app</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Add the </span><code class=""><span>CardPayments</span></code><span> package dependency for your app using </span><strong><span>Swift Package Manager</span></strong><span> or </span><strong><span>CocoaPods</span></strong><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><h4>Swift Package Manager</h4><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Open Xcode.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/swift_packages/adding_package_dependencies_to_your_app" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Follow the guide</span></a><span> to add package dependencies to your app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Enter </span><a href="https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class=""><span>https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/</span></code></a><span> as the repository URL.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the checkbox for the </span><code class=""><span>CardPayments</span></code><span> framework.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><h4>CocoaPods</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Include </span><code class=""><span>PayPal/CardPayments</span></code><span> in your Podfile:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
    </span><div><span>
        </span><div class="copyBtn-wrapper"><span>
            </span><span>
        </span></div><span>
        </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"># </span><span class="token maybe-class-name">Podfile</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">pod </span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&#x27;PayPal/CardPayments&#x27;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
    </span></div><span>
</span></div><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><h3>2. Create CardClient</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A </span><code class=""><span>CardClient</span></code><span> helps you attach a card to a payment.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>In your iOS app:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Use the </span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_ID</span></code><span> to construct a </span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Construct a </span><code class=""><span>CardClient</span></code><span> using your </span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span> object.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><div class="codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
    </span><div><span>
        </span><div class="copyBtn-wrapper"><span>
            </span><span>
        </span></div><span>
        </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21"     </span></div><span>
</span></div><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><h3>3. Get Order ID</h3><span>
</span><p><span>On your server:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Create an </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span> by using the </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Pass your </span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span> in the </span><code class=""><span>Authorization</span></code><span> header. To get an </span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span>, use the </span><a href="/api/rest/authentication/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Authentication API</span></a><span>.</span><span class="warning"><br/></span><span>
        </span><p><span class="warning"><strong><span>Note:</span></strong><span> This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to </span></span><a href="https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
        </span><p></p><span>
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Pass the </span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span>. You'll need to pass either </span><code class=""><span>AUTHORIZE</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>CAPTURE</span></code><span> as the </span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span> type. This type must match the </span><code class=""><span>/authorize</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>/capture</span></code><span> endpoint you use to process your order.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><h4>Sample request</h4><span>

</span><p></p><span>
</span><p><span>When a buyer starts a payment, send the </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span> from your server to your client app.</span></p><span>
</span><h3>4. Create card request</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> object:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Attaches a card to an </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Launches 3D Secure when a payment requires additional authentication.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><h4>1. Collect card payment details</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Build a </span><code class=""><span>card</span></code><span> object with the buyer's card details:</span></p><span>

data-testid="lineNumber">12</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token literal-property property">postalCode</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">:</span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;12345&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
    </span></div><span>
</span></div><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><p><span>Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.</span></p><span>
</span><h4>2. Build CardRequest</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Build a </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> with the </span><code class=""><span>card</span></code><span> object and your </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>

</span><div class="codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
    </span><div><span>
        </span><div class="copyBtn-wrapper"><span>
            </span><span>
        </span></div><span>
        </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token keyword" style="color:rgb(86, 156, 214)">let</span><span class="token plain"> cardRequest </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">CardRequest</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token literal-property property">orderID</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">:</span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;ORDER_ID&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">3</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token literal-property property">card</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">:</span><span class="token plain"> card</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">4</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token literal-property property">sca</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">:</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">.</span><span class="token property-access">scaAlways</span><span class="token comment" style="color:rgb(106, 153, 85)">// default value is .scaWhenRequired</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">5</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
    </span></div><span>
</span></div><span>
</span><p><a href="/api/nvp-soap/payflow/3d-secure-overview/" target="_blank"><span>3D Secure</span></a><span> is supported for all card payments to comply with the </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/uk/webapps/mpp/PSD2?_ga=1.18434873.1625369690.1652045188" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Second Payment Services Directive (PSD2)</span></a><span>. PSD2 is a European Union regulation that introduces </span><a href="https://www.ukfinance.org.uk/our-expertise/payments-and-innovation/strong-customer-authentication" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Strong Customer Authentication (SCA)</span></a><span> and other security requirements.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Select your SCA launch option type using the </span><code class=""><span>sca</span></code><span> parameter in the </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> initializer:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>SCA.scaWhenRequired</span></code><span> launches an SCA challenge when applicable. This is enabled by default.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>SCA.scaAlways</span></code><span> requires an SCA challenge for all card transactions.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><h3>5. Approve order</h3><span>
</span><p><span>After your </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> has the card details, call </span><code class=""><span>cardClient.approveOrder()</span></code><span> to process the payment.</span></p><span>

successfully</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl"     </span></div><span>
</span></div><span>

</span><h3>7. Authorize and capture order</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Submit your </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span> for authorization or capture when the PayPal iOS SDK calls the </span><code class=""><span>didFinishWithResult</span></code><span> method.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Call the </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class=""><span>authorize</span></code></a><span> endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:</span></p><span>
</span><h4>Sample request: Authorize order</h4><span>



</span><div class="codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
    </span><div><span>
        </span><div class="copyBtn-wrapper"><span>
            </span><span>
        </span></div><span>
        </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">curl --location --request POST &#x27;https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize&#x27; \</span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">  -H &#x27;Content-Type: application/json&#x27; \</span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">3</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">  -H &#x27;Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN&#x27; \</span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">4</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">  --data-raw &#x27;&#x27;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
    </span></div><span>Call the </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class=""><span>capture</span></code></a><span> endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:
</span></div><span>

</span></div><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><h3>8. Test integration</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Before going live, test your integration in the </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/" target="_blank"><span>sandbox environment</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Learn more about the following resources on the </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Card Testing</span></a><span> page:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Use </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testcardnumbers" target="_blank"><span>test card numbers</span></a><span> to simulate successful payments for advanced checkout integrations.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Use </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-rejectiontriggers" target="_blank"><span>rejection triggers</span></a><span> to simulate card error scenarios.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Test </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-simulate3dsecurecardpayments" target="_blank"><span>3D Secure authentication</span></a><span> scenarios.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Test your integration by following </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testintegration" target="_blank"><span>these recommended use cases</span></a><span>. See the </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span> for details about billing address fields and other parameters. For example, use the </span><a href="/api/rest/reference/country-codes/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>2-character country code</span></a><span> to test the billing address.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="margin-left:30px"><strong><span>Note:</span></strong><span> Use the </span><a href="/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-creditcardgenerator" target="_blank"><span>credit card generator</span></a><span> to generate additional test credit cards for sandbox testing.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><p><span>When prompted for required data for the sandbox business request, such as a phone number, enter any number that fits the required format. Because this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Before you go live, you'll need to complete </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/entry/product/ppcp" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>live onboarding</span></a><span> to be eligible to process cards with your live PayPal account.</span></p><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="payment-buttons-and-fraud-protection" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="payment-buttons-and-fraud-protection" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#payment-buttons-and-fraud-protection" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#payment-buttons-and-fraud-protection" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Payment buttons and fraud protection</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>After you integrate a payment method, add a payment button to your page to start the payment process. id="panel-Payment buttons" class="tab-panel-margin css-1kheh2r-tabs_content-tabs_content_focus-tab_content_visible" aria-labelledby="Payment buttons" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="0" role="tabpanel" data-ppui="true"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div style="background-color:rgb(250,248,251)"><span>
</span><h2>Use PayPal buttons in your UI</h2><span>
</span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>PaymentButtons</span></code><span> module provides a set of PayPal-branded buttons to seamlessly integrate with PayPal </span><code class=""><span>web</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>native</span></code><span> payments.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Follow these steps to add PayPal buttons to your integration:</span></p><span>
</span><h3>1. Add PaymentButtons to your app</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Add the </span><code class=""><span>PaymentButtons</span></code><span> package dependency for your app using </span><strong><span>Swift Package Manager</span></strong><span> or </span><strong><span>CocoaPods</span></strong><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><h4>Swift Package Manager</h4><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Open Xcode.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/swift_packages/adding_package_dependencies_to_your_app" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Follow the guide</span></a><span> to add package dependencies to your app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Enter </span><a href="https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class=""><span>https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/</span></code></a><span> as the repository URL.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the checkbox for the </span><code class=""><span>PaymentButtons</span></code><span> framework.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><h4>CocoaPods</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Include </span><code class=""><span>PayPal/PaymentButtons</span></code><span> in your Podfile:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="codeBlocks-wrapper"><div><div class="copyBtn-wrapper"></div><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"># </span><span class="token maybe-class-name">Podfile</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">pod </span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&#x27;PayPal/PaymentButtons&#x27;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div></div></div><span>

</span><h3>2. Create PayPal button</h3><span>
</span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>PaymentButtons</span></code><span> module provides 3 buttons that you can use in your application:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>PayPalButton</span></code><span>: A generic PayPal button.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>PayPalPayLater</span></code><span>: A PayPal button with a PayLater label.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>PayPalCredit</span></code><span>: A PayPal button with the PayPalCredit logo.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><span>These buttons include customization options such as color, shape, size, and labels. Here's how to style the button corner radius:</span></p><span>
</span><style data-emotion="css 16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100{color:#001435;font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,"Helvetica Neue",Arial,sans-serif;font-size:1.125rem;line-height:1.5rem;font-weight:400;border-spacing:0;border-collapse:separate;text-align:start;width:100%;}@media screen and (max-width: 752px){.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100{font-size:min(1.125rem, 36px);line-height:min(1.5rem, 48px);}}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr{background-color:#ffffff;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr >td,.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr >th{border-bottom:0.0625rem solid #929496;border-top:0.0625rem solid transparent;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr >td{padding:0.75rem;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr >td:first-of-type{padding-left:1rem;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr Card Payments in iOS Apps | PayPal Developer","description":"Accept PayPal, credit, debit card payments in your iOS app with customizable buttons \u0026 UI. Easily integrate with PayPal Mobile iOS SDK for seamless experience."},"language":["en-US"],"ecm":{"link":"https://internal.paypalinc.com/contentmanager/space/b7241346-cd3d-4e70-a1c7-74bfd4aaab3d/environment/ddea4eb4-f0c4-4321-aa67-654e40fe9a18/entries/2Erv0NNMOm26W8VCooBYCW","envAllowsPreview":true},"markdownContent":"---\ntitle: Integrate card payments in iOS apps\nslug: /docs/checkout/advanced/ios/\ncreateTime: '2024-07-18T05:45:34.203Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-05-12T10:31:15.108Z'\n---\n\n\n# Integrate card payments in iOS apps\n\nIn certain countries, Apple allows apps to link to an external website for processing payments. Use these guides to learn on how to enable this type of flow using PayPal.\n\nPlease refer to this repository for sample integration: [https://github.com/paypal-examples/paypal-ios-sdk-demo-app](https://github.com/paypal-examples/paypal-ios-sdk-demo-app)\n\n\nAccept PayPal, credit, and debit card payments in a web or native experience using the PayPal Mobile iOS SDK. Use customizable PayPal buttons with your custom checkout UI to align with your business branding. For more implementation details, see the [PayPal GitHub repository](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/) .\n\n\n\n## Know before you code \n\n### You need a developer account to get sandbox credentials\nPayPal uses the following REST API credentials, which you can get from the developer dashboard:\n\n- **Client ID** : Authenticates your account with PayPal and identifies an app in your sandbox.\n- **Client secret** : Authorizes an app in your sandbox. Keep this secret safe and don't share it.\n\n\n### You'll need both PayPal and third-party tools\nYou need a combination of PayPal and third-party tools:\n\n- [iOS SDK](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/) : Adds PayPal-supported payment methods for iOS.\n- [Orders REST API](/docs/api/orders/v2/) : Create, update, retrieve, authorize, and capture orders.\n\n\n### Explore PayPal APIs with Postman\n\n\nYou can use Postman to explore and test PayPal APIs. Learn more in our [Postman guide](/api/rest/postman) .\n\n\n\n## Before you begin \n### Check your account setup for advanced card payments\nThis integration requires a sandbox business account with the Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments capability. Your account should automatically have this capability.\n\nTo confirm that Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments are enabled for you, check your sandbox business account as follows:\n\n- Log into the [**PayPal Developer Dashboard**](/dashboard/) , toggle **Sandbox** , and go to **Apps \u0026 Credentials** .\n- In **REST API apps** , select the name of your app.\n- Go to **Features** \u0026gt; **Accept payments** .\n- Select the **Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments** checkbox and select **Save Changes** .\n\n\n**info**\n**Note:** If you created a sandbox business account through [sandbox.paypal.com](https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/?_ga=1.158343865.248280996.1670866755) , and the advanced credit and debit card payments status for the account is disabled, [complete the sandbox onboarding steps](https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/bizsignup/#/checkAccount) .\n\n\n### Check 3D Secure requirements\nAdd 3D Secure to reduce the chance of fraud and improve the payment experience by authenticating a cardholder through their card issuer.\n\nVisit our [3D Secure](/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/3d-secure/) page to see if 3D Secure is required in your region and learn more about implementing 3D Secure in your app.\n\n\n\n## Integrate the SDK into your app \nIntegrate 3 different types of payments using the PayPal Mobile SDK:\n\n- **Card payments:** Add card fields that align with your branding.\n- **PayPal native payments:** Launch a checkout page within your app, instead of a popup.\n- **PayPal web payments:** A lighter integration that launches a checkout page in a browser within your app.\n\n\n### Card\n## Integrate with card payments\nBuild and customize the card fields to align with your branding.\n\n### 1. Add card payments module to your app\nAdd the CardPayments package dependency for your app using **Swift Package Manager** or **CocoaPods** :\n\n#### Swift Package Manager\n- Open Xcode.\n- [Follow the guide](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/swift_packages/adding_package_dependencies_to_your_app) to add package dependencies to your app.\n- Enter [https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/) as the repository URL.\n- Select the checkbox for the CardPayments framework.\n\n#### CocoaPods\nInclude PayPal/CardPayments in your Podfile:\n\n1#Podfile2pod'PayPal/CardPayments'\n\n### 2. Create CardClient\nA CardClient helps you attach a card to a payment.\n\nIn your iOS app:\n\n- Use the CLIENT_ID to construct a CoreConfig .\n- Construct a CardClient using your CoreConfig object.\n\n1letcoreConfig=CoreConfig(clientID:\"CLIENT_ID\",environment:.sandbox)2letcardClient=CardClient(config:coreConfig)\n\n### 3. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an ORDER_ID by using the [Orders v2 API](/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your ACCESS_TOKEN in the Authorization header. To get an ACCESS_TOKEN , use the [Authentication API](/api/rest/authentication/) .    **Note:**This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n  \n\n \n- Pass the intent . You'll need to pass either AUTHORIZE or CAPTURE as the intent type. This type must match the /authorize or /capture endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n#### Sample request\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw '{5\"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",6\"purchase_units\": [7{8\"amount\": {9\"currency_code\": \"USD\",10\"value\": \"5.00\"11}12}13]14}'\n\n#### Sample response\n1{2\"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",3\"status\":\"CREATED\"4}\n\nWhen a buyer starts a payment, send the ORDER_ID from your server to your client app.\n\n### 4. Create card request\nA CardRequest object:\n\n- Attaches a card to an ORDER_ID .\n- Launches 3D Secure when a payment requires additional authentication.\n\n#### 1. Collect card payment details\nBuild a card object with the buyer's card details:\n\n1letcard=Card(2number:\"4005519200000004\",3expirationMonth:\"01\",4expirationYear:\"2025\",5securityCode:\"123\",6cardholderName:\"Jane Smith\",7billingAddress:Address(8addressLine1:\"123 Main St.\",9addressLine2:\"Apt. 1A\",10locality:\"City\",11region:\"IL\",12postalCode:\"12345\",13countryCode:\"US\"14)15)\n\nCollecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.\n\n#### 2. Build CardRequest\nBuild a CardRequest with the card object and your ORDER_ID :\n\n1letcardRequest=CardRequest(2orderID:\"ORDER_ID\",3card:card,4sca:.scaAlways// default value is .scaWhenRequired5)[3D Secure](/api/nvp-soap/payflow/3d-secure-overview/) is supported for all card payments to comply with the [Second Payment Services Directive (PSD2)](https://www.paypal.com/uk/webapps/mpp/PSD2?_ga=1.18434873.1625369690.1652045188) . PSD2 is a European Union regulation that introduces [Strong Customer Authentication (SCA)](https://www.ukfinance.org.uk/our-expertise/payments-and-innovation/strong-customer-authentication) and other security requirements.\n\nSelect your SCA launch option type using the sca parameter in the CardRequest initializer:\n\n- SCA.scaWhenRequired launches an SCA challenge when applicable. This is enabled by default.\n- SCA.scaAlways requires an SCA challenge for all card transactions.\n\n### 5. Approve order\nAfter your CardRequest has the card details, call cardClient.approveOrder() to process the payment.\n\n1classMyViewController:UIViewController{2funccardCheckoutTapped(cardRequest:CardRequest){3cardClient.approveOrder(request:cardRequest)4}5}\n\n### 6. Handle payment result scenarios\nSet up your CardDelegate to handle successful payments, errors, cancellations, and 3D Secure transaction flows.\n\n1extensionMyViewController:CardDelegate{2funcsetupCardClient(){3cardClient.delegate=self4}5// MARK: - CardDelegate6funccard(_ cardClient:CardClient,didFinishWithResult result:CardResult){7// Order was approved and is ready to be captured/authorized (refer to the next step)8}9funccard(_ cardClient:CardClient,didFinishWithError error:CoreSDKError){10// handle the error by accessing `error.localizedDescription`11}12funccardDidCancel(_ cardClient:CardClient){13// 3D Secure auth was canceled by the user14}15funccardThreeDSecureWillLaunch(_ cardClient:CardClient){16// 3D Secure auth will launch17}18funccardThreeDSecureDidFinish(_ cardClient:CardClient){19// 3D Secure auth did finish successfully20}21}### 7. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your ORDER_ID for authorization or capture when the PayPal iOS SDK calls the didFinishWithResult method.\n\nCall the [authorize](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize) endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''Call the[capture](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture)endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:#### Sample request: Capture order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''\n\n### 8. Test integration\nBefore going live, test your integration in the [sandbox environment](/tools/sandbox/) .\n\nLearn more about the following resources on the [Card Testing](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/) page:\n\n- Use [test card numbers](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testcardnumbers) to simulate successful payments for advanced checkout integrations.\n- Use [rejection triggers](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-rejectiontriggers) to simulate card error scenarios.\n- Test [3D Secure authentication](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-simulate3dsecurecardpayments) scenarios.\n- Test your integration by following [these recommended use cases](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testintegration) . See the [Orders v2 API](/docs/api/orders/v2/) for details about billing address fields and other parameters. For example, use the [2-character country code](/api/rest/reference/country-codes/) to test the billing address.\n\n**Note:** Use the [credit card generator](/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-creditcardgenerator) to generate additional test credit cards for sandbox testing.\n\nWhen prompted for required data for the sandbox business request, such as a phone number, enter any number that fits the required format. Because this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.\n\nBefore you go live, you'll need to complete [live onboarding](https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/entry/product/ppcp) to be eligible to process cards with your live PayPal account.\n\n\n,### Native payments\n## Use PayPal native payments\n**Deprecation notice: ThePayPalNativePaymentsmodule has been deprecated since July 2024. Updates and bug fixes will end in July 2025. We recommend to use thePayPalWebPaymentsmodule instead. To migrate fromPayPalNativePaymentstoPayPalWebPayments, follow the steps in the Web Payments tab.**\n\nUse PayPalNativePayments to add a PayPal paysheet to your app. The paysheet is a checkout page that the client launches within your app, instead of showing up as a pop-up. The paysheet shows all the PayPal payment methods available and helps the payer complete their payment.\n\n### Native checkout for a first-time customer\n  \n\n![checkout,for,a,first-time,customer,steps,1,to,3](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_01.png)\n\n![checkout,for,a,first-time,customer,steps,4,to,6](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_02.png) \n\n### Native checkout for a returning customer\n  \n\n![checkout,for,a,returning,customer](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-repeat-time-flow.png)\n\n  \n\nFollow these steps to add PayPalNativePayments :\n\n### 1. Add PayPalNativePayments module to your app\nAdd the PayPal/PayPalNativePayments package dependency for your app using **Swift Package Manager** or **CocoaPods** :\n\n#### Swift Package Manager\n\n\n- Open Xcode.\n- [Follow the guide](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/swift_packages/adding_package_dependencies_to_your_app) to add package dependencies to your app.\n- Enter [https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/) as the repository URL.\n- Select the checkbox for the PayPalNativePayments framework.\n\n\n\n#### CocoaPods\n1#Podfile2pod'PayPal/PayPalNativePayments'\n\n### 2. Enable Native Checkout SDK\nYou'll need to set up authorization to use the Native Checkout SDK. To create a client ID and secret, follow the steps in [Get Started](/api/rest/#link-getstarted) . You need these values to generate an ACCESS_TOKEN .\n\nSet up your sandbox business account to use native checkout as follows:\n\n- Log into the [**PayPal Developer Dashboard**](/dashboard/) , toggle **Sandbox** , and go to **Apps \u0026 Credentials** .\n- In **REST API apps** , select the name of your app.\n- Go to **Features** \u0026gt; **Accept payments** and select ***Native Checkout SDK** .\n- Select **Save Changes** .\n\n**Note:** This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n### 3. Create PayPalNativeCheckoutClient\nUse the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:\n\n#### 1. Construct CoreConfig\nIn your iOS app, use the CLIENT_ID to construct a CoreConfig .\n\n1letconfig=CoreConfig(clientID:\"CLIENT_ID\",environment:.sandbox)\n\n#### 2. Create native checkout request\nCreate a PayPalNativeCheckoutClient request to approve an order with a PayPal payment method:\n\n1letpayPalNativeClient=PayPalNativeCheckoutClient(config:config)\n\n#### 3. Set up payment delegate\nSet a PayPalNativeCheckoutDelegate to listen for result notifications from the SDK:\n\n1extensionMyViewController:PayPalNativeCheckoutDelegate{2funcpaypal(_ payPalClient:PayPalNativeCheckoutClient,didFinishWithResult approvalResult:Approval){3// order was approved and is ready to be captured/authorized (see step 5)4}5funcpaypal(_ payPalClient:PayPalNativeCheckoutClient,didFinishWithError error:CoreSDKError){6// handle the error by accessing `error.localizedDescription`7}8funcpaypalDidCancel(_ payPalClient:PayPalNativeCheckoutClient){9// the user canceled10}11funcpaypalWillStart(_ payPalClient:PayPalNativeCheckoutClient){12// the PayPal paysheet is about to show up. Handle loading views, spinners, etc.13}14}#### 4. Listen for shipping details\nWhen a payer chooses to use shipping details from their PayPal profile, use PayPalNativeShippingDelegate to listen for changes to their shipping address or shipping method.\n\nYou can only implement PayPalNativeShippingDelegate if the [shipping_preference](/docs/api/orders/v2/#definition-experience_context_base) in the order ID is set to GET_FROM_FILE.\n\n**Note:** Skip this step if you created your order ID with shipping_preference set to NO_SHIPPING or SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS .\n\nSet a shippingDelegate on the PayPalNativeCheckoutClient to send notifications to your app when the user updates their shipping address or shipping method.\n\n1extension MyViewModel: PayPalNativeShippingDelegate {2func setup() {3paypalNativeClient.delegate = self         // always required4paypalNativeClient.shippingDelegate = self // required for `GET_FROM_FILE` orders5}6func paypal(7_ payPalClient: PayPalNativeCheckoutClient,8didShippingAddressChange shippingAddress: PayPalNativeShippingAddress,9withAction shippingActions: PayPalNativePaysheetActions10) {11// called when the user updates their chosen shipping address12// you must call shippingActions.approve() or shippingActions.reject() in this callback13shippingActions.approve()14// OPTIONAL: you can optionally patch your order. Once complete, call shippingActions.approve() if successful or shippingActions.reject() if not.15}16func paypal(17_ payPalClient: PayPalNativeCheckoutClient,18didShippingMethodChange shippingMethod: PayPalNativeShippingMethod,19withAction shippingActions: PayPalNativePaysheetActions20) {21// called when the user updates their chosen shipping method22// patch your order server-side with the updated shipping amount.23// Once complete, call `shippingActions.approve()` or `shippingActions.reject()`24if patchOrder() == .success {25shippingActions.approve()26} else {27shippingActions.reject()28}29}30}#### 5. Modify shipping details\nWhen the shipping method changes, update the order details on your server by sending a PATCH request to the [Update order](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch) endpoint of the Orders API.\n\nApprove or reject changes to the shipping information to see changes appear in the paysheet UI by calling either PayPalNativePaysheetActions.approve() or PayPalNativePaysheetActions.reject() .\n\nTo update the paysheet with a new shipping method, or when didShippingMethodChange is called:\n\n- Patch the order on your server using the replace operation with all shipping methods. - Mark the new shipping method as selected.\n- Optional: Update the amount to reflect the new shipping cost.\n\n \n- Call approve() or reject() to accept or reject the changes and continue the payment flow.\n\nFor more information, visit the [Update order](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch) endpoint of the Orders v2 API.\n\n### 4. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an ORDER_ID by using the [Orders v2 API](/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your ACCESS_TOKEN in the Authorization header. To get an ACCESS_TOKEN , use the [Authentication API](/api/rest/authentication/) . **Note:** This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n \n- Pass the intent . You'll need to pass either AUTHORIZE or CAPTURE as the intent type. This type must match the /authorize or /capture endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n#### Sample request\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw '{5\"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",6\"purchase_units\": [7{8\"amount\": {9\"currency_code\": \"USD\",10\"value\": \"5.00\"11}12}13]14}'#### Sample response\n1{2\"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",3\"status\":\"CREATED\"4}\n\nWhen a buyer starts a payment, send the ORDER_ID from your server to your client app.\n\n### 5. Start PayPal Native Payments flow\nTo start the PayPal Native Payments flow, call the startCheckout function in PayPalNativeCheckoutClient , with a PayPalNativeCheckoutRequest :\n\n1letrequest=PayPalNativeCheckoutRequest(orderID:\"ORDER_ID\")2paypalNativeClient.start(request:request)### 6. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your ORDER_ID for authorization or capture when the PayPal iOS SDK calls the onPayPalSuccess method.\n\nCall the [authorize](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize) endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''Call the [capture](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture) endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:\n\n#### Sample request: Capture order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''\n,### Web payments\n## PayPal Web Payments\nIntegrate PayPalWebPayments to add a lighter checkout integration to your app. The checkout experience is launched in a browser within your application, reducing the size of the SDK.\n\nFollow these steps to integrate PayPalWebPayments :\n\n### 1. Add PayPalWebPayments to your app\nAdd the PayPalWebPayments package dependency for your app using **Swift Package Manager** or **CocoaPods** :\n\n#### Swift Package Manager\n- Open Xcode.\n- [Follow the guide](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/swift_packages/adding_package_dependencies_to_your_app) to add package dependencies to your app.\n- Enter [https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-ios/) as the repository URL.\n- Select the checkbox for the PayPalWebPayments framework.\n\n#### CocoaPods\nInclude PayPal/PayPalWebPayments in your Podfile:\n\n1#Podfile2pod'PayPal/PayPalWebPayments'### 2. Create PayPalWebCheckoutClient\nUse the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:\n\n#### 1. Construct CoreConfig\nIn your iOS app, use the CLIENT_ID to construct a CoreConfig .\n\n1letconfig=CoreConfig(clientID:\"CLIENT_ID\",environment:.sandbox)#### 2. Create web checkout request\nCreate a PayPalWebCheckoutClient to approve an order with a PayPal payment method:\n\n1letpayPalClient=PayPalWebCheckoutClient(config:config)### 3. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an ORDER_ID by using the [Orders v2 API](/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your ACCESS_TOKEN in the Authorization header. To get an ACCESS_TOKEN , use the [Authentication API](/api/rest/authentication/) . **Note:** This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n \n- Pass the intent . You'll need to pass either AUTHORIZE or CAPTURE as the intent type. This type must match the /authorize or /capture endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n#### Sample request\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw '{5\"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",6\"purchase_units\": [7{8\"amount\": {9\"currency_code\": \"USD\",10\"value\": \"5.00\"11}12}13]14}'#### Sample response\n1{2\"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",3\"status\":\"CREATED\"4}When a buyer starts a payment, send the ORDER_ID from your server to your client app.\n\n**Note:** Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.\n\n### 4. Create web checkout request\nConfigure your PayPalWebCheckoutRequest with the ORDER_ID . You can also specify one of the following funding sources for your order: PayPal (default), PayLater , or PayPalCredit .\n\n1letpayPalWebRequest=PayPalWebCheckoutRequest(orderID:\"ORDER_ID\",fundingSource:.paypal)### 5. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your ORDER_ID for authorization or capture when the PayPal iOS SDK calls the onPayPalWebSuccess method on PayPalWebCheckoutListener .\n\nCall the [authorize](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize) endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''Call the [capture](/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture) endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:\n\n#### Sample request: Capture order\n1curl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\2-H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\3-H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\4--data-raw ''\n\n\n## Payment buttons and fraud protection \nAfter you integrate a payment method, add a payment button to your page to start the payment process. You can also add fraud protection to your app.\n\n\n### Payment buttons\n## Use PayPal buttons in your UI\nThe PaymentButtons module provides a set of PayPal-branded buttons to seamlessly integrate with PayPal web and native payments.\n\nFollow these steps to add PayPal buttons to your integration:\n\n### 1. Create PayPal button\nThe PaymentButtons module provides 3 buttons that you can use in your application:\n\n- PayPalButton : A generic PayPal button.\n- PayPalPayLater : A PayPal button with a PayLater label.\n- PayPalCredit : A PayPal button with the PayPalCredit logo.\n\nThese buttons include customization options such as color, shape, size, and labels. Here's how to style the button corner radius:\n\n| Value | Description | Button |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| rectangle | Button shape with sharp corners. |\n| rounded | **Recommended** Button shape with rounded corner radius. The default button shape. |  |\n| pill | Button in pill shape. |  |\n| custom(CGFloat) | Customize the button's corner radius. The minimum value is 10 px and is applied to all 4 corners. |\n\nAdd buttons using either UKit or SwiftUI as follows:\n\n#### UKit\n1class MyViewController: UIViewController {2lazy var payPalButton: PayPalButton = {3let payPalButton = PayPalButton()4payPalButton.addTarget(self, action: #selector(payPalButtonTapped), for: .touchUpInside)5return payPalButton6}()7@objc func payPalButtonTapped() {8// Insert your code here9}10override func viewDidLoad() {11super.viewDidLoad()12view.addSubview(payPalButton)13}14}#### SwiftUI\n1struct MyApp: View {2@ViewBuilder3var body: some View {4VStack {5PayPalButton.Representable() {6// Insert your code here7}8}9}10}\n,### Fraud protection\n## Protect from fraud\nThe FraudProtection module helps you collect data about a customer's device and match it with a session identifier on your server. For more information, see [Fraud protection](/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/fraud-protection/) .\n\n### 1.
